Service: Atour's service is probably the most considerate I have ever stayed in. I usually live in Hyatt, Kempinski and the like. Breakfast, the variety of breakfast is okay for the price, the display of things is exquisite, and the restaurant is petty bourgeoisie. Not much, definitely enough to eat. Eat until the end of breakfast. Atour can only guarantee good food and fullness. It is definitely not a place to eat all the time.
Disadvantages, I think the only disadvantage is that the house is too small and requires staff to open the windows. You said that I want to find you when I open, and I want to find you when Guan. I would feel very embarrassed, so I just didn't open it. But I will feel uncomfortable.
